| <span data-ttu-id="93a76-457">Eingabe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93a76-457">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93a76-458">Wert</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93a76-458">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="93a76-1703">Bemerkungen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93a76-1703">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93a76-1704">Die **MS-DFSR-replicationgroup-** Klasse ist Teil der Unterstützung für den verteiltes Dateisystem (DFS)-Replikations Dienst.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93a76-1704">The **ms-DFSR-ReplicationGroup** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
